AGRICULTURE DEPARTMENT
Secretariat, 22nd  November 2017.
No. II(2)/AG/970/2017.
[Agriculture - Notiﬁ cation of Districts and Revenue villages for Paddy II (Samba/Thaladi/Pishanam) 2017 season 
under Pradhan Mantri Fasal Bima Yojana and publication in the State Government Gazette - Orders - issued.]
The following Government order is published:—
[G.O. Ms. No. 209, Agriculture (AP6), 22nd August 2017, Ýõí¤ 6,   
«ýM÷‹H, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2048.]
                                                           
READ:

G.O.(Ms).No.123,   Agriculture (AP6) Department,   dated 5.5.2017
2. 
G.O.(Ms).No.135,   Agriculture (AP6) Department,   dated 24.5.2017.
3. 
G.O.(D).No.176,   Agriculture (AP6) Department,    dated 27.6.2017.
4. 
Minutes of the State Level Coordination Committee on Crop Insurance (SLCCCI) Special Meeting conducted 
on 24.7.2017.
5. 
From the Director of Agriculture Letter No.G1/71997/2017,   dated  5.8.2017 and 10.8.2017.
6. 
Government Letter No.19159/AP6/2017-1,   dated 9.8.2017.
ORDER No. 209,   Agriculture (AP6),   22nd August 2017.
 In the Government Order second read above,   the Government have  accorded administrative approval for 
implementation of Pradhan Mantri Fasal Bima Yojana (PMFBY) at an outlay of Rs.522.70 crore in all the districts of 
Tamil Nadu except Chennai during 2017-2018 as per the Administrative approval and operational guidelines of “Pradhan 
Mantri Fasal Bima Yojana” (PMFBY).


2
2. In the Government Order ﬁ rst read above, orders were issued for notiﬁ cation of crops, districts, ﬁ rkas, revenue 
villages, insurance units and approved premium rates for Agricultural and Horticultural Crops for Kharif 2017 under 
“Pradhan Mantri Fasal Bima Yojana”.
3. In the Government Order third read above, the Government have notiﬁ ed the Scale of Finance approved for 
2017-2018 as sum insured for the crops notiﬁ ed during 2017-2018 under “Pradhan Mantri Fasal Bima Yojana”.
4. In his letter ﬁ fth read above, the Director of Agriculture has informed that as the Sowing Season for Paddy 
– II (Samba / Thaladi / Pishanam) commences in the month of August and prolongs upto November and the sowing 
of Paddy-II crop is taken up both in Kharif & Rabi, Paddy II has to be notiﬁ ed in advance under “Pradhan Mantri 
Fasal Bima Yojana” before the commencement of the season. This was accepted in the 38th State Level Coordination 
Committee on Crop Insurance meeting held on 30.3.2017 and accordingly a State Level Coordination Committee on Crop 
Insurance Special meeting was conducted on 24.07.2017 under the Chairmanship of Agricultural Production Commissioner 
and Principal Secretary to Government, Agriculture Department to notify Paddy – II (Samba / Thaladi / Pishanam) during 
2017-2018. The Committee has ﬁ nalized the insurance units and approved premium rates and accepted for notiﬁ cation.
5. The Director of Agriculture has therefore sent proposals for notiﬁ cation of Paddy II (Samba / Thaladi / Pishanam) 
during the year 2017-2018 and requested to issue orders on the following:-
 
i. 
For notiﬁ cation of Paddy II crop and the Insurance units (revenue villages) under Paddy II crop; 
 
ii. 
For approval of the Implementing Agencies (Insurance Company) and implementation of the scheme in 
the three clusters;
 
iii. 
To adopt the approved Premium Rates for Paddy II for the year 2017-2018; 
 
iv. 
To ﬁ x the Indemnity Level for the purpose of calculation of Threshold yield at 90% for low risk districts, 
80% for medium risk districts and 70% for high risk districts; 
 
v. 
To ﬁ x the seasonality / cut-off date for Paddy II as 30th November, 2017; 
 
vi. 
To authorize the District Level Monitoring Committee under the Chairmanship of District Collector to ﬁ x 
the seasonality discipline for 2017-2018 for prevented sowing / failed sowing besides notifying the Post harvest losses 
at farm level and invoking mid-season adversity for on-account payment as done during 2016-2017; 
 
vii. Publication of notiﬁ cation in the Government Gazette;
6. The Government,   after careful examination of the proposal of the Director of Agriculture accept the same and accordingly 
hereby notify (1) Paddy II crop (Samba / Thaladi / Pishanam), (2) District wise approved premium rates for Paddy – II and 
(3) Cluster wise, District wise Insurance units (Revenue Villages) during 2017-2018 under Pradhan Mantri Fasal Bima 
Yojana as shown in the Annexures I, II and III respectively to this order.
7. 
The Government also direct that –
 
(i) discrepancies if any noted in the hierarchy of the notiﬁ ed units at any stage of implementation of the scheme 
during enrollment,   implementation / uploading in Government of India portal / while processing of compensation shall 
be reconciled by the Insurance Companies with the Department of Economics and Statistics and the hierarchy ﬁ xed by 
Department of Economics and Statistics shall be adopted as ﬁ nal;
 
(ii) the claims under the Pradhan Mantri Fasal Bima Yojana Scheme shall be settled on the basis of yield data 
furnished by the Department of Economics and Statistics as per prescribed cut-off dates for the notiﬁ ed crops / districts 
/ ﬁ rkas / revenue villages for the effective implementation of Pradhan Mantri Fasal Bima Yojana scheme for Paddy II 
(Samba/Thaladi/Pishanam) season and not on the basis of the Annavari Certiﬁ cate / Gazette notiﬁ cation declaring the 
area as Drought / Flood / Cyclone affected etc., by the District Collectors;
 
(iii) the District Level Monitoring Committee under the Chairmanship of District Collector is authorised to ﬁ x 
the seasonality discipline for 2017-2018 for prevented sowing / failed sowing besides notifying the Post harvest losses 
at farm level and invoking mid-season adversity for on-account payment as done during 2016-2017;
 (By Order of the Governor)


3
PRADHAN MANTRI FASAL BIMA YOJANA (PMFBY)
NOTIFICATION FOR PADDY- II DURING 2017 -2018
ANNEXURE I 
(G.O.Ms.No.209,   Agriculture (AP6) Department,   dated 22.8.2017)
Pradhan Mantri Fasal Bima Yojana (PMFBY) will be implemented in all districts of Tamil Nadu (except Chennai) 
with the State Government subsidy during 2017-2018 for Paddy II (Samba / Thaladi / Pishanam). 
I. 
OBJECTIVES:
Pradhan Mantri Fasal Bima Yojana aims at supporting sustainable production in agriculture by way of 
a) 
Providing ﬁ nancial support to farmers suffering crop loss/damage arising out of unforeseen events.
b) 
Stabilizing the income of farmers to ensure their continuance in farming.
c) 
Encouraging farmers to adopt innovative and modern Agriculture practices.
d) 
Ensuring ﬂ ow of credit to the agriculture sector, which will, contribute to food security, crop diversiﬁ cation and 
enhancing growth and competitiveness of agriculture sector besides protecting farmers from production risks.
II. 
COVERAGE OF FARMERS:
All farmers including share croppers and tenant farmers growing the notiﬁ ed crops in the notiﬁ ed areas are eligible 
for coverage.
· 
Compulsory to loanee farmers.
· 
Optional for non - loanee farmers.
III. COVERAGE OF RISKS AND EXCLUSIONS:
1. 
PREVENTED SOWING/ PLANTING RISK - Insured area is prevented from sowing / planting due to deﬁ cit 
rainfall or adverse seasonal conditions and non release of irrigation water on scheduled date of opening of dam for 
irrigation in its command areas.
2. 
STANDING CROP (SOWING TO HARVESTING) - Comprehensive risk insurance is provided to cover yield 
losses due to non - preventable risks viz. Drought, dry spells, ﬂ ood, inundation, pests and diseases, landslides, natural 
ﬁ re and lightening, storm, hailstorm, cyclone, typhoon, tempest, hurricane and tornado. 
3. 
POST-HARVEST LOSSES - Coverage against speciﬁ c perils of cyclone, cyclonic rains and unseasonal rains is 
available only upto a maximum period of two weeks from harvesting, for those crops which are allowed to dry in cut 
and spread condition in the ﬁ eld after harvesting. 
4. 
LOCALIZED CALAMITIES - Loss/damage resulting due to occurrence of identiﬁ ed localized risks viz., hailstorm, 
landslide and inundation affecting isolated farms in the notiﬁ ed area. 
In the Special State Level Coordination Committee on Crop Insurance meting conducted for notiﬁ cation of Paddy II 
on 24.07.2017, the Committee has authorized the District Level Monitoring Committee under the Chairmanship of District 
Collector to ﬁ x the seasonality discipline for prevented sowing/failed sowing and Post harvest losses at farm level and 
mid-season adversity for on-account payment (vide G.O.Ms.No.293 Agriculture (AP6) Department, dated 12.9.2016) as 
done during 2016-2017. 
Sl.
No.
Localized Perils
Districts Notiﬁ ed

4
IV. SUM INSURED:
The Sum Insured per hectare for Paddy notiﬁ ed vide G.O.(D).No.176,   Agriculture (AP6) Department,   dated 
27.6.2017 shall be adopted and will be the same for both loanee and non-loanee farmers. 
V. PREMIUM RATE AND PREMIUM SUBSIDY:
FARMER’S PREMIUM: 
Actuarial Premium Rate (APR) would be charged under Pradhan Mantri Fasal Bima Yojana by the Implementing 
Agency (IA). The rate of Insurance Charges for Paddy II (Samba/Thaladi/Pishanam) payable by the farmer is 1.5% of 
Sum Insured or Actuarial rate,   whichever is less .
VI. SEASONALITY DISCIPLINE/ CUT-OFF DATE:
The seasonality / cut-off date for Paddy II (Samba/Thaladi/Pishanam) cultivated during August 2017 to January 2018 
is ﬁ xed as 30th November,   2017.

IX. INDEMNITY LEVEL FOR THE PURPOSE OF CALCULATION OF THRESHOLD YIELD:
The Indemnity Level for the purpose of calculation of Threshold yield at 90% for low risk districts,   80% for medium risk 
districts and 70% for high risk districts
